<h1 id="portals-api-beta-">Portals API (BETA)</h1> <p><strong>This API is in beta testing and may be subject to the occasional tweak. Any such tweaks will be documented here.</strong></p> <p>Portals provides a user authentication and management system on top of the One Platform. The Portals API provides access to Portals functionality using a REST-style HTTP API, using the JSON format in request and response bodies, and basic authentication where a Portals account is required.</p> <h2 id="overview">Overview</h2> <p>Below are some documents that will help you understand the basics of all Portals API.</p> <ul> <li><a href="#api-endpoints">API Endpoints</a></li> <li><a href="#api-index">API Index</a></li> <li><a href="#rest">REST</a></li> <li><a href="#request-and-response-format">Request and Response Format</a></li> <li><a href="#delete-domain-widget">/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</a></li> <li>[GET] <a href="#get-domain-widget">/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</a></li> <li>[GET] <a href="#update-domain-widget">/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</a></li> </ul> <h2 id="rest">REST</h2> <p>The API uses a REST-style API, which means that:</p> <ul> <li>HTTP verbs in the request indicate the type of action the client wants to take (e.g. GET, POST)</li> <li>HTTP status in the response indicate (e.g. 200 for success, 400 for bad request or 401 for authentication error)</li> </ul> <h2 id="request-and-response-format">Request and Response Format</h2> <p>Request and response bodies, when present, are formatted using JSON. For more see <a href="http://json.org">http://json.org</a></p> <p>Note that the JSON examples below are sometimes formatted with extra whitespace for clarity.</p> <p>The header MUST include:</p> <pre><code>Content-type: application/json; charset=utf-8 </code></pre><h2 id="authentication">Authentication</h2> <p>Some API endpoints require a Portals email and password also username and password to combination for authentication. These are passed using basic access authentication. See this link for details about this method of authentication:</p> <p><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basic_access_authentication">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basic_access_authentication</a></p> <h2 id="definition-of-domain">Definition of domain</h2> <p>For some API endpoints, the domain of the request URL indicates information about which domain should be affected. For example, a GET request to:</p> <pre><code>https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portal/ </code></pre><p>...will return a different array of portals than a GET request to:</p> <pre><code>https://portals.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portal/ </code></pre><p>Also, the domain is used for user authentication. Endpoints that are affected by the querying domain are indicated below.</p> <h2 id="objects">Objects</h2> <p>The following objects are common to several API endpoints.</p> <h3 id="account-object">Account object</h3> <p>An object containing information about a Portals user.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;email&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;id&quot;: &lt;id&gt;, &quot;rid&quot;:&lt;rid&gt;, &quot;meta&quot;: &lt;meta&gt;, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;userName&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s email address. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;fullName&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s full name. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is a numeric identifier for the user.</li> <li><code>&quot;meta&quot;</code> may be any type. It contains application-specific information describing the user. It MUST be less than 2 megabytes long when it is serialized to a JSON string.</li> <li><code>&quot;phoneNumber&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s phone number. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;userName&quot;</code> is a string identifier for the user. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> </ul> <h3 id="client-model-object">Client model object</h3> <p>A sample client model object looks like this:</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;id&quot;: &quot;samplevendor\/samplemodel&quot;, &quot;domainID&quot;: &quot;0000000000&quot;, &quot;vendor&quot;: &quot;samplevendor&quot;, &quot;friendly&quot;: &quot;dfhg&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;samplemodel&quot;, &quot;cloneRID&quot;: &quot;29770f4f96122ffd33af1f6edb1b875810c7844a&quot;, &quot;viewID&quot;: &quot;0000000000&quot;, &quot;exampleSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;sharedSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;convertSN&quot;: &quot;no&quot;, &quot;alternateSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteSetup&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteLocation&quot;: &quot;(optional - can be a string or GPS decimal degrees)&quot;, &quot;pictureDevice&quot;: &quot;https:\/\/portals.yourdomain.com\/cache\/model\/samplevendor\/samplemodel_PictureDevice.png&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;pictureSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;confirmPage&quot;: &quot;Your [client model name] [device] was successfully enabled with the CIK\u003Cbr\/\u003E[device cik]\u003Cbr\/\u003E\u003Cbr\/\u003EYour [device] will need to connect to the Exosite platform within 24 hours or your provision request will expire and you will need to re-enable your [device] from the Re-Enable block in your [device] pop-up. If you have any problems connecting, please contact your [device] provider at:\u003Cbr\/\u003E\u003Cbr\/\u003E\u003Cb\u003ECompany name:\u003C\/b\u003E [company name]\u003Cbr\/\u003E\u003Cb\u003ECompany email contact information:\u003C\/b\u003E [company email]\u003Cbr\/\u003E&quot;, &quot;companyName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;contactEmail&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;:published&quot;: true } </code></pre><h3 id="dashboard-object">Dashboard object</h3> <p>A sample dashboard object.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;config&quot;: object = { &quot;layout&quot; : object = { &quot;cols&quot;: 2 | 4 | 6 = 4, &quot;gravity&quot;: &quot;LeftTop&quot; | &quot;Top&quot; = &quot;LeftTop&quot; }, &quot;widgets&quot;: object = {} }, &quot;description&quot;: string = &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: string, &quot;location&quot;: string = &quot;&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: string, &quot;portalId&quot;: string, &quot;public&quot;: boolean = false } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;config&quot;</code> is dashboard configuration which is limited to 16MB characters.<ul> <li><code>&quot;layout&quot;</code> is dashboard layout.<ul> <li><code>&quot;cols&quot;</code> means 1 column by 2 grids, e.g. 2 columns equal to 4 grids.</li> <li><code>&quot;gravity&quot;</code> provides dashboard layout alignment.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;widgets&quot;</code> provides each widget configuration on the dashboard.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> is dashboard description which is limited to 255 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is a 10 digit dashboard identifier.</li> <li><code>&quot;location&quot;</code> is dashboard location which is limited to 255 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> is a descriptive name which is limited to 50 characters and must be unique under corresponding portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;portalId&quot;</code> is a 10 digit identifier of portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;public&quot;</code> provides public read-only access. If set to true, it makes the dashboard readable by any user. If set to false, the dashboard is readable only by any user who has dashboard view or portal manage permission.</li> </ul> <h3 id="data-source-object">Data source object</h3> <p>A data source object describes a Portals time series data source.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;data&quot;: [ [ &lt;unix-timestamp-1&gt;, &lt;value-1&gt; ], [ &lt;unix-timestamp-2&gt;, &lt;value-2&gt; ], ... ], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;basic&quot;: &lt;basic&gt;, &quot;description&quot;: &lt;description&gt;, &quot;shares&quot;: &lt;shares&gt;, &quot;storage&quot;: &lt;storage&gt;, &quot;subscribers&quot;: &lt;subscribers&gt;, &quot;tags&quot;: &lt;tags&gt; }, &quot;rid&quot;: &lt;rid&gt;, &quot;unit&quot;: &lt;unit&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><p><code>&quot;data&quot;</code> is an array of data points. A data point has a unit timestamp and a value.</p> <ul> <li><p><code>&lt;unix-timestamp-N&gt;</code> is a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix_time">Unix timestamp</a>, measured in number of seconds since the epoch.</p> </li> <li><p><code>&lt;value-N&gt;</code> may be a string, int, or float depending on the data source type.</p> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;info&quot;</code> is a dataport object documented in the <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#info">remote procedure call documentation</a>. But only basic, description, shares, storage, subscribers and tags are exposed.</p> </li> <li><code>&quot;rid&quot;</code> is the RID of a data source.</li> <li><code>&quot;unit&quot;</code> is the unit of a data source.</li> </ul> <h3 id="device-object">Device object</h3> <p>A device object describes a device in Portals.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;dataSources&quot;: [ &lt;data-source-rid-1&gt;, &lt;data-source-rid-2&gt;, ... ], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;aliases&quot;: &lt;aliases&gt;, &quot;basic&quot;: &lt;basic&gt;, &quot;description&quot;: &lt;description&gt;, &quot;key&quot;: &lt;key&gt;, &quot;shares&quot;: &lt;shares&gt;, &quot;subscribers&quot;: &lt;subscribers&gt;, &quot;tagged&quot;: &lt;tagged&gt;, &quot;tags&quot;: &lt;tags&gt;, }, &quot;members&quot;: [ &lt;permission-1&gt;, &lt;permission-2&gt;, ... ], &quot;model&quot;: &lt;model-id&gt;, &quot;rid&quot;: &lt;rid&gt;, &quot;sn&quot;: &lt;sn&gt;, &quot;type&quot;: &lt;device-type&gt;, &quot;vendor&quot;: &lt;vendor-id&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><p><code>&quot;dataSources&quot;</code> is an array of data source IDs a device has.</p> <ul> <li><code>&lt;data-source-rid-N&gt;</code> is a 40 character hex string representing the data source&#39;s RID in the One Platform</li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;info&quot;</code> is an client object documented in the <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#info">remote procedure call documentation</a>. But only aliases, basic, description, key, shares, subscribers, tagged and tags are exposed.</p> <ul> <li><code>&lt;key&gt;</code> is a 40 character hex string representing the client&#39;s CIK in the One Platform or null if the authorized user doesn&#39;t have ___admin permission to this device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;members&quot;</code> is an array of <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> listing the members of the device.</p> </li> <li><code>&quot;model&quot;</code> is a string identifying the model</li> <li><code>&quot;rid&quot;</code> is the RID of a device.</li> <li><code>&quot;sn&quot;</code> is a string representing the serial number of the device</li> <li><p><code>&quot;type&quot;</code> is a constant string representing the device type. Possible values are:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;vendor&quot;</code></li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;vendor-id&quot;</code> is a string identifying the vendor</p> </li> </ul> <h3 id="domain-widget-object">Domain widget object</h3> <p>A sample domain widget object.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;code&quot;: &quot;function(){}&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;no operation&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;0000000000&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;noop&quot; } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;code&quot;</code> is JavaScript code of domain widget. It MUST be less than 1 megabyte after serializing to JSON.</li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> is description of domain widget. It MUST be less than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is identifier of domain widget.</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> is name of domain widget. It MUST be less than or euqal to 50 characters.</li> </ul> <h3 id="group-object">Group object</h3> <p>A group object describes a Portals permissions group.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;id&quot;: &lt;group-id&gt;, &quot;members&quot;: [ &lt;permission-1&gt;, ... ], &quot;meta&quot;: &lt;meta&gt;, &quot;name&quot;: &lt;short-text&gt;, &quot;permissions&quot;: [ &lt;permission-1&gt;, ... ], &quot;userId&quot;: &lt;user-id&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is a number identifying the group.</li> <li><code>&quot;members&quot;</code> is an array of <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> listing the members of the group.</li> <li><code>&quot;meta&quot;</code> may be any type. It contains application-specific information describing the group. It MUST be less than 2 megabytes long when it is serialized to a JSON string.</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> is the group name. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters. It MUST be unique among the same user in a domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;permissions&quot;</code> is an array of <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> describing Portals resources members of the group may access.</li> <li><code>&quot;userId&quot;</code> is a number identifying the owner of the group.</li> </ul> <h3 id="permission-object">Permission object</h3> <p>A permission object describes a level of access to a particular Portals resource identified by <code>&quot;oid&quot;</code>, and is filtered by current domain of its resource, which means a permission list never contains resources which not belong to current domain.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;access&quot;: &lt;access&gt;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;id&quot;: &lt;id&gt;, &quot;type&quot;: &lt;type&gt; } } </code></pre><ul> <li><p><code>&quot;access&quot;</code> is a string to define what the permission owner has. Possible values are:</p> <p><code>&quot;___admin&quot;</code> (Default) means the owner has the highest permission to the resources.</p> <ul> <li><p>Common Access</p> <ul> <li><p>Dashboard</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;v___view&quot;</code> means the owner can get the dashboard information.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Data Sources</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;d__write&quot;</code> means the owner can get the data source information, and read, write data to data source.</li> <li><code>&quot;d___read&quot;</code> means the owner can get the data source information, and read data from data source.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Device</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;d_update&quot;</code> means the owner can get, update the decvice information and delete the device.</li> <li><code>&quot;d___view&quot;</code> means the owner can get device information.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Domain</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;d_s_cont&quot;</code> means the owner can update the domain information.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_s_crea&quot;</code> means the owner can create a group to the domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_p_list&quot;</code> means the owner can create a portal to the domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_p_crea&quot;</code> means the owner can just create a portal to himself.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_u_list&quot;</code> means the owner can get user, get users list, and delete user form the domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_u_view&quot;</code> means the owner can get user, get users list form the domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;d_____fs&quot;</code> means the owner can create, update and delete the file systems in the domain.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Group</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;g_update&quot;</code> means the owner can modifying member list of the group and read, update the group information.</li> <li><code>&quot;g_member&quot;</code> means the owner can modifying member list of the group and read the group information.</li> <li><code>&quot;g_modera&quot;</code> means the owner can modifying member list of the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Portal</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;p_manage&quot;</code> means the owner can get, update portal information and create device, data source to the portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_m_crea&quot;</code> means the owner can create device to the portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p___view&quot;</code> means the owner can get portal information, get device and get data source under the portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_contac&quot;</code> means the owner can receive alerts from the portal.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;oid&quot;</code> is an object identifying the resource with the permission.</p> <ul> <li><p><code>&lt;id&gt;</code> is a number identifying the resource.</p> </li> <li><p><code>&lt;type&gt;</code> is a string identifying the thing to which the permission provides access. It may have one of the following values:</p> <ul> <li><p><code>&quot;DataSource&quot;</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;Device&quot;</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;Domain&quot;</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;Group&quot;</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;Portal&quot;</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;User&quot;</code></p> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h4 id="example">Example</h4> <ul> <li>Update user permission</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_update&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Device&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;dc226acdf0f9b92e40f0f62878970417b8689f9e&quot;}}]}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:33:44 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;updatedemail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_update&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Device&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;dc226acdf0f9b92e40f0f62878970417b8689f9e&quot;}}] } </code></pre><ul> <li>Update group permission</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/3167859736&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_update&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Device&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;dc226acdf0f9b92e40f0f62878970417b8689f9e&quot;}}]}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:33:44 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;updatedemail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_update&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Device&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;dc226acdf0f9b92e40f0f62878970417b8689f9e&quot;}}] } </code></pre><h3 id="portal-object">Portal object</h3> <p>An object containing information about a portal.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;devices&quot;: [ &lt;device-rid-1&gt;, &lt;device-rid-2&gt;, ... ], &quot;id&quot;: &lt;id&gt;, &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;aliases&quot;: &lt;aliases&gt;, &quot;basic&quot;: &lt;basic&gt;, &quot;description&quot;: &lt;description&gt;, &quot;key&quot;: &lt;key&gt;, &quot;shares&quot;: &lt;shares&gt;, &quot;subscribers&quot;: &lt;subscribers&gt;, &quot;tagged&quot;: &lt;tagged&gt;, &quot;tags&quot;: &lt;tags&gt;, }, &quot;planId&quot;: &lt;plan-id&gt;, } </code></pre><ul> <li><p><code>&quot;devices&quot;</code> is an array of identifiers for devices of which the portal owns.</p> <ul> <li><code>&lt;device-rid-N&gt;</code> is a 40 character hex string representing the device&#39;s RID in the One Platform</li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is a numeric identifier for the portal.</p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;info&quot;</code> is an client object documented in the <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#info">remote procedure call documentation</a>. But only aliases, basic, description, key, shares, subscribers, tagged and tags are exposed.</p> <ul> <li><code>&lt;key&gt;</code> is a 40 character hex string representing the client&#39;s CIK in the One Platform or null if the authorized user doesn&#39;t have ___admin permission to this portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;planId&quot;</code> is a numeric identifier for the plan of the portal.</p> </li> </ul> <h3 id="script-object">Script object</h3> <p>A sample script object.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;rid&quot;: &lt;rid&gt;, &quot;data&quot;: &lt;data&gt;, &quot;info&quot;: &lt;info&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&lt;rid&gt;</code> is a 40 digit resource identifier.</li> <li><code>&lt;data&gt;</code> is a list of timestamp, value pairs.</li> <li><code>&lt;info&gt;</code> is information about an existing resource.</li> </ul> <h3 id="theme-object">Theme object</h3> <p>A sample theme object looks like this:</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3077881923&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;sample_theme&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;this is a description&quot;, &quot;:default&quot;: true, &quot;config&quot;: { &quot;dashboard_background&quot;: { &quot;background_color&quot;: &quot;F9F9F9&quot;, &quot;background_image&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;background_attachment&quot;: &quot;scroll&quot;, &quot;background_repeat&quot;: &quot;repeat-y&quot;, &quot;background_position&quot;: &quot;left top&quot; }, &quot;header_logo&quot;: &quot;https:\/\/portals.yourdomain.com\/cache\/theme\/0_1923506535_header_logo.png&quot;, &quot;header_bkimage&quot;: &quot;https:\/\/portals.yourdomain.com\/static\/png\/skin_portals_bannerbg.png?62d38477d5d7a46968a168c460bf76fc&quot;, &quot;header_title_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;header_subtitle_color&quot;: &quot;FFFFFF&quot;, &quot;header_titles_position_top&quot;: &quot;1.375em&quot;, &quot;header_linktext_color&quot;: &quot;E5E5E5&quot;, &quot;header_linktextover_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;header_dropdown_text_color&quot;: &quot;FFFFFF&quot;, &quot;header_linktext_position_top&quot;: &quot;1.5em&quot;, &quot;header_portalmenu_current_color&quot;: &quot;0000FF&quot;, &quot;footer_text&quot;: &quot;ANY DEVICE. ANY DATA. ANY WHERE.&quot;, &quot;footer_text_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;footer_bar_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;footer_linktext_color&quot;: &quot;5C5D60&quot;, &quot;footer_linktextover_color&quot;: &quot;000000&quot;, &quot;block_title_text_color&quot;: &quot;000000&quot;, &quot;block_title_linkover_color&quot;: &quot;010101&quot;, &quot;block_title_back_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;block_invert_icons&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;managepage_highlight_text_color&quot;: &quot;0000FF&quot;, &quot;dashboard_thumbnail&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;thankyoupage_title_text_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot;, &quot;browser_tab_text&quot;: &quot;Exosite Portals&quot;, &quot;browser_tab_icon&quot;: &quot;https:\/\/portals.yourdomain.com\/static\/png\/icon_exosite.png?834282e60aa5c2cf2d3a6894307437dd&quot;, &quot;admin_menu_style&quot;: { &quot;admin_menu_title&quot;: &quot;Domain Admin&quot;, &quot;manage_menu_title&quot;: &quot;Manage&quot;, &quot;secondary_menu_title&quot;: &quot;Portal Menu&quot;, &quot;account_menu_title&quot;: &quot;Account&quot;, &quot;menu_title_color&quot;: &quot;E5E5E5&quot;, &quot;background_color&quot;: &quot;5C5D60&quot;, &quot;background_hover_color&quot;: &quot;A6A6A6&quot;, &quot;text_color&quot;: &quot;FFFFFF&quot;, &quot;sub_background_color&quot;: &quot;FFFFFF&quot;, &quot;sub_background_hover_color&quot;: &quot;A6A6A6&quot;, &quot;sub_text_color&quot;: &quot;5C5D60&quot;, &quot;text_active_color&quot;: &quot;D5E04D&quot; }, &quot;jsCode&quot;: &quot;&quot; }, &quot;code&quot;: &quot;&quot; } </code></pre><h3 id="user-object">User object</h3> <p>An object containing information about a Portals user.</p> <pre><code>{ &quot;activated&quot;: &lt;boolean&gt;, &quot;email&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;groups&quot;: [ &lt;group-id-1&gt;, &lt;group-id-2&gt;, ... ], &quot;id&quot;: &lt;id&gt;, &quot;meta&quot;: &lt;meta&gt;, &quot;permissions&quot;: [ &lt;permission-1&gt;, ... ], &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt;, &quot;userName&quot;: &lt;short-string&gt; } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;activated&quot;</code> indicates whether a user is activated in the domain or not.</li> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s email address. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;fullName&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s full name. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><p><code>&quot;groups&quot;</code> is an array of identifiers for groups of which the user is a member.</p> <ul> <li><code>&lt;group-id-N&gt;</code> is a number identifying the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> is a numeric identifier for the user.</p> </li> <li><code>&quot;meta&quot;</code> may be any type. It contains application-specific information describing the user. It MUST be less than 2 megabytes long when it is serialized to a JSON string.</li> <li><code>&quot;permissions&quot;</code> is an array of <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> describing Portals resources the user may access.</li> <li><code>&quot;phoneNumber&quot;</code> is the user&#39;s phone number. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> <li><code>&quot;userName&quot;</code> is a string identifier for the user. It is a string of fewer than 256 characters.</li> </ul> <h3 id="user-id">User ID</h3> <p>Anywhere an API endpoint takes a user ID, you can instead use _this as an alias for the user ID of the authenticated user.</p> <h4 id="example">Example</h4> <p>Given a request is authenticated as a user with ID being 1234.</p> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/1234</code></p> <p>yields the same result as</p> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/_this</code></p> <h2 id="caveats">Caveats</h2> <p>API return messages may be subject to upgrades and improvements (e.g., additional fields may be added). Developers using Exosite APIs should not hard code non-upwards-compatible elements such as field counts, IP addresses, or header length.</p> <h2 id="resources">Resources</h2> <h3 id="accounts">Accounts</h3> <h4 id="get-all-user-accounts">Get all user accounts</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/accounts</code></p> <blockquote> <p><strong>Deprecated.</strong> This API is deprecated and should not be used.</p> </blockquote> <p>Get account information about all users.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#account-object">account object</a> if the caller user has permission to list accounts.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have <code>d_u_view</code> permission for the domain.</li> <li><code>500 Internal Server Error</code>: Returned if an error occurs while retrieving the list of accounts.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/accounts&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:42:30 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;useremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;7fe862bd9f274b8ab80cf22284a2316599024fb9&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;userName&quot;:&quot;useremail&quot; }, { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3407735538&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;7fe862bd9f274b8ab80cf22284a2316599024fb0&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;userName&quot;:&quot;existinguseremail&quot; }, ... ] </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-account-by-email">Get user account by email</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/accounts/{user-email}</code></p> <p>Get user account information by email.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own account information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an <a href="#account-object">account object</a> if the caller user has permission to get account and the callee user exists in the domain.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the callee user does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/accounts/existinguseremail@gmail.com&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:40:58 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 99 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3407735538&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;7fe862bd9f274b8ab80cf22284a2316599024fb0&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;userName&quot;:&quot;existinguseremail&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-account-by-user-id">Get user account by user ID</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/accounts/{user-id}</code></p> <p>Get user account by user ID.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own account information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an <a href="#account-object">account object</a> if the caller user has permission to get account and the callee user exists in the domain.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the callee user does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/accounts/3407735538&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:40:58 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 99 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3407735538&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;7fe862bd9f274b8ab80cf22284a2316599024fb0&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;userName&quot;:&quot;existinguseremail&quot; } </code></pre><h3 id="client-models">Client Models</h3> <p>Client models represent a class of devices. All devices of the same client model have the same behaviour attributes and pricing. Only the domain administrator can use the client model APIs. <strong>Note: Image data can currently not be modified using this API</strong></p> <h4 id="get-client-model">Get client model</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/client-models/{vendor}/{name}</code></p> <p>Get information about a client model.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#client-model-object">client model object</a> if the caller user has permission to get client models and the client model exists in the domain.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get client model.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the client model does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/client-models/myvendor/myname&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:21:14 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 1071 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;id&quot;: &quot;myvendor/myname&quot;, &quot;domainID&quot;: &quot;3481377489&quot;, &quot;vendor&quot;: &quot;myvendor&quot;, &quot;friendly&quot;: &quot;myname&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;myname&quot;, &quot;cloneRID&quot;: &quot;96436ca6874ce01d0dd1f41001d71e75c3aebd6f&quot;, &quot;viewID&quot;: &quot;0000000000&quot;, &quot;exampleSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;sharedSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;convertSN&quot;: &quot;no&quot;, &quot;alternateSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteSetup&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;noteLocation&quot;: &quot;(optional - can be a string or GPS decimal degrees)&quot;, &quot;pictureDevice&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;pictureSN&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;confirmPage&quot;: &quot;Your [client model name] [device] was successfully enabled with the CIK&lt;br/&gt;[device cik]&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;Your [device] will need to connect to the Exosite platform within 24 hours or your provision request will expire and you will need to re-enable your [device] from the Re-Enable block in your [device] pop-up. [company email]&lt;br/&gt;&quot;, &quot;companyName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;contactEmail&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;:published&quot;: false } </code></pre><h4 id="update-client-model">Update client model</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/client-models/{vendor}/{name}</code></p> <p>Update information about a client model.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a JSON encoded <a href="#client-model-object">client model object</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the client model is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update client model.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the client model does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/client-models/myvendor/mymodel&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;description&quot;: &quot;sample model&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 08:14:01 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="list-client-models">List client models</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/client-models/</code></p> <p>Returns an array of client models in this domain.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#client-model-object">client models object</a> if the caller user has permission to list client models.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to list client models.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the client model does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/client-models&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:10:30 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; &quot;:published&quot;: true }, ... ] </code></pre><h4 id="delete-client-model">Delete client model</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/client-models/{vendor}/{name}</code></p> <p>When deleting the current default client model the exosite system client model will be applied to the domain.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the client model is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete client model.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the client model does not exist in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/client-models/myvendor/mymodel&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:26:52 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="get-serial-number">Get serial number</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/client-models/{vendor}/{name}/sn/{serial-number}</code></p> <p>Get information about a serial number.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to device with the serial number ( Set &quot;Allow customer to use the API to get the Serial Number extra field.&quot; from admin/configuration page.)</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a JSON entity. if the caller user has permission to get serial number.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get serial number.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the serial number does not be used.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/client-models/myvendor/mymodel/sn/123&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;domainuseremail@gmail.com:adminuserPassword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:10:30 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;status&quot;: &quot;expired&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;847699a4667a64a42eaca6ecd0f564374e64b9f7&quot;, &quot;extra&quot;: &quot;test for extra info&quot;, } </code></pre><h3 id="collections-bulk-request-">Collections (bulk request)</h3> <h4 id="get-multiple-data-sources">Get multiple data sources</h4> <p><code>GET /users/_this/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]</code></p> <p>Get information for data sources.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___read</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Internal limit is 200 some are smaller.<br>0 &lt;= x &lt;= (INTERNAL LIMIT).</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Numbers of items to skip.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]?offset=10</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if the caller user has permission to get data sources.</li> <li><code>206 Partial Content</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if request ID is over the response limit, link will appear in header <code>Link=&lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;previous&quot;, &lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;next&quot;</code>.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get data sources.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if one of callee data sources is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <h6 id="if-all-items-are-fetched">If all items are fetched</h6> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/data-sources/\[a3fc4e5a6fbc20fcb14091ba0735580e56060e9a,a90f263111b05088a3c78aef511f14275bba6cc5\]&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 02:49:17 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 648 Content-Type: /users/_this/devices/[{device-rid},{device-rid},...]</code></p> <p>Get information for devices.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the devices.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Internal limit is 200 some are smaller.<br>0 &lt;= x &lt;= (INTERNAL LIMIT).</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{device-rid},{device-rid},...]?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Numbers of items to skip.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{device-rid},{device-rid},...]?offset=10</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if the caller user has permission to get devices.</li> <li><code>206 Partial Content</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if request ID is over the response limit, link will appear in header <code>Link=&lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;previous&quot;, &lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;next&quot;</code>.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if one of callee devices is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get devices.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <h6 id="if-all-items-are-fetched">If all items are fetched</h6> <pre><code>curl groups.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>g_member</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the groups.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Internal limit is 200 some are smaller.<br>0 &lt;= x &lt;= (INTERNAL LIMIT).</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{group-id},{group-id},...]?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Numbers of items to skip.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{group-id},{group-id},...]?offset=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>NoPermissions</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The response object will not include permission items.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{group-id},{group-id},...]?NoPermissions</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#group-object">group object</a> if the caller user has permission to get groups.</li> <li><code>206 Partial Content</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#group-object">group object</a> if request ID is over the response limit, link will appear in header <code>Link=&lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;previous&quot;, &lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;next&quot;</code>.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get groups.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <h6 id="if-all-items-are-fetched">If all items are fetched</h6> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/groups/\[2581071857,2937453355\]&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{user-id},{user-id},...]?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Numbers of items to skip.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{user-id},{user-id},...]?offset=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>NoPermissions</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The response object will not include permission items.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/_this/users/[{user-id},{user-id},...]?NoPermissions</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the caller user has permission to get users.</li> <li><code>206 Partial Content</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if request ID is over the response limit, link will appear in header <code>Link=&lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;previous&quot;, &lt;{url}&gt;; rel=&quot;next&quot;</code>.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get users.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <h6 id="if-all-items-are-fetched">If all items are fetched</h6> <pre><code>curl id="create-portal-dashboard">Create portal dashboard</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}/dashboards</code></p> <p>Create portal dashboard.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p_manage</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <pre><code>{ &quot;config&quot;: object = &lt;config&gt;, &quot;description&quot;: string = &quot;&quot;, &quot;location&quot;: string = &quot;&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: string, &quot;public&quot;: boolean = false } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&quot;config&quot;</code> See <a href="#dashboard-object">dashboard object</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#dashboard-object">dashboard object</a> if the dashboard is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create dashboard under the portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if portal id is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if the dashboard name exists already.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/1284862590/dashboards&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;Demo&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;domainuseremail@gmail.com:adminuserP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Thu, 14 May 2015 10:14:23 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: &quot;description&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3087021266&quot;, &quot;location&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;Demo&quot;, &quot;portalId&quot;: &quot;1284862590&quot;, &quot;public&quot;: false } </code></pre><h4 id="delete-dashboard">Delete dashboard</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/dashboards/{dashboard-id}</code></p> <p>Delete dashboard.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the dashboard.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the dashboard is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete the dashboard.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the dashboard id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl caller user has permission to get dashboard information.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get dashboard information.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> /api/portals/v1/dashboards/{dashboard-id}</code></p> <p>Update dashboard.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;config&quot;: { &quot;layout&quot;: { &quot;cols&quot;: 4, &quot;gravity&quot;: &quot;LeftTop&quot; }, &quot;widgets&quot;: [] }, &quot;1284862590&quot;, &quot;public&quot;: false } </code></pre><h3 id="data-sources">Data Sources</h3> <h4 id="create-portal-data-source">Create portal data source</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}/data-sources</code></p> <p>Create a data source inside a portal</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p_manage</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a>. Currently only the following keys are supported:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;format&quot;</code> - Data source format under info description.(optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - Data source name under info description.(optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;unit&quot;</code> - Data source unit under info description.(optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if the data source is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create data sources for the portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/2853566858/data-sources&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;:{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;: &quot;new data&quot;}}}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:25:20 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 452 Content-Type: application/json; }, &quot;subscribe&quot;: null }, &quot;shares&quot;: [], &quot;storage&quot;: { &quot;count&quot;: 0, &quot;first&quot;: 0, &quot;last&quot;: 0, &quot;size&quot;: 0 }, &quot;subscribers&quot;: [], &quot;tags&quot;: [] }, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f&quot;, &quot;unit&quot;: &quot;&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="update-data-source">Update data source</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-sources-rid}</code></p> <p>Update a data sources.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data source.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;info&quot;: {&quot;description&quot;: ...}</code> - description under info (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if the data source is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update data sources.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;: {&quot;description&quot;: {&quot;name&quot;: &quot;data source update name&quot;}}}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 06 Jan 2015 03:25:15 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 565 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;data&quot;: [ [1413958187, &quot;1413519694&quot;] ], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;basic&quot;: { &quot;modified&quot;: 1420514686, &quot;subscribers&quot;: 0, &quot;type&quot;: &quot;dataport&quot; }, &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;format&quot;: &quot;string&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: &quot;{\&quot;datasource\&quot;:{\&quot;description\&quot;:\&quot;test\&quot;,\&quot;unit\&quot;:\&quot;1413519694\&quot;},\&quot;alias\&quot;:\&quot;1413519694\&quot;}&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;data source update name&quot;, &quot;preprocess&quot;: [], &quot;public&quot;: true, &quot;retention&quot;: { &quot;count&quot;: &quot;infinity&quot;, &quot;duration&quot;: &quot;infinity&quot; }, &quot;subscribe&quot;: null }, &quot;shares&quot;: [], &quot;storage&quot;: { &quot;count&quot;: 1, &quot;first&quot;: 1413958187, &quot;last&quot;: 1413958187, &quot;size&quot;: 14 }, &quot;subscribers&quot;: [], &quot;tags&quot;: [&quot;test&quot;] }, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f&quot;, &quot;unit&quot;: &quot;1413519694&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="create-device-data-source">Create device data source</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/devices/{device-rid}/data-sources</code></p> <p>Create a data source under a device.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the device.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a object. Currently only the following keys are supported:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;info&quot;</code> - Data source info. (optional)<ul> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> - Data source description. (optional)<ul> <li><code>&quot;format&quot;</code> - Data source format. (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - Data source name. (optional)</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;unit&quot;</code> - Data source unit. (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if the data source is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create data sources for the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/devices/bbc295c0dc98f8518b784867bae4a1b168c77f1b/data-sources&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Mon, 13 Apr 2015 07:30:18 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 451 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;data&quot;: [], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;basic&quot;: { &quot;modified&quot;: 1428910043, &quot;subscribers&quot;: 0, &quot;type&quot;: &quot;dataport&quot; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="get-data-source">Get data source</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}</code></p> <p>Get information about a Portals data source. If you want to get more than one data source information can reference <a href="#get-multiple-data-sources">Get multiple data sources</a>.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___read</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#data-source-object">data source object</a> if the caller user has permission to get data source information.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get data source information.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f&#39;
