}, &quot;subscribe&quot;: null }, &quot;shares&quot;: [], &quot;storage&quot;: { &quot;count&quot;: 0, &quot;first&quot;: 0, &quot;last&quot;: 0, &quot;size&quot;: 0 }, &quot;subscribers&quot;: [], &quot;tags&quot;: [] }, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f&quot;, &quot;unit&quot;: &quot;&quot; } </code></pre><h3 id="data-sources-data">Data Sources Data</h3> <h4 id="get-data-source-data">Get data source data</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___read</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <p>This API can retrieve multiple data points. The options below can be included to modify the results of an API call:</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>starttime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the start time of window to read.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?starttime=1416278080</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>endtime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the end time of window to read.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?endtime=1416278417</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>sort</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Defines the order in which points should be ordered: ascending (<code>&quot;asc&quot;</code>) or descending (<code>&quot;desc&quot;</code>) timestamp order.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?sort=desc</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Sets a maximum on the number of data points to return.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?limit=2</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>For more details about these options, see the <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#read">read API</a>.</p> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the caller user has permission to get data source data, and along with an array of <code>&quot;data&quot;</code> contents like following:<ul> <li><code>&quot;data&quot;</code> is an array of data points. A data point has a unit timestamp and a value.<ul> <li><code>{unix-timestamp}</code> is a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix_time">Unix timestamp</a>, measured in number of seconds since the epoch.</li> <li><code>{value}</code> may be a string, int, or float depending on the data source type.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get data source data.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Get data with no option</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/data&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:39:23 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 21 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [[1416278080,&quot;1000&quot;]] </code></pre><ul> <li>Get data with options</li> </ul> <p>api/portals/v1/data-sources/<code>ResourceID</code>/data?starttime=<code>Unix Timestamp for starttime</code>&amp;endtime=<code>Unix Timestamp for endtime</code>&amp;limit=<code>Number of data points</code>&amp;sort=<code>Sorting order of choice</code></p> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/data?starttime=1416278080&amp;endtime=1416278417&amp;limit=2&amp;sort=desc&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:43:35 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 41 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [[1416278417,&quot;5.00&quot;],[1416278080,&quot;1000&quot;]] </code></pre><h4 id="get-data-source-data-bulk-request">Get data source data bulk request</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___read</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <p>This API can retrieve multiple data points. The options below can be included to modify the results of an API call:</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>starttime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the start time of window to read.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?starttime=1416278080</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>endtime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the end time of window to read.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data?endtime=1416278417</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>sort</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Defines the order in which points should be ordered: ascending (<code>&quot;asc&quot;</code>) or descending (<code>&quot;desc&quot;</code>) timestamp order.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?sort=desc</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Sets a maximum on the number of data points to return.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?limit=2</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>For more details about these options, see the <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#read">read API</a>.</p> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the caller user has permission to get data source data, and along with a JSON object contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>{data-source-rid}</code> is an array of data points from the data source. A data point has a unit timestamp and a value.<ul> <li><code>{unix-timestamp}</code> is a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix_time">Unix timestamp</a>, measured in number of seconds since the epoch.</li> <li><code>{value}</code> may be a string, int, or float depending on the data source type.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get data source data.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Get data with no option</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/\[3218552df19a93a3f1b85c29fd0f46ddff2f7071,437240fba025d3416a60ef1a160e5424d4138fdc\]/data&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 10:22:30 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 {&quot;3218552df19a93a3f1b85c29fd0f46ddff2f7071&quot;:[],&quot;437240fba025d3416a60ef1a160e5424d4138fdc&quot;:[]} </code></pre><h4 id="append-data-source-data">Append data source data</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d__write</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a <a href="#data-source-object">value</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned if the data is appended to data source successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission append data to the data source.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/data&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;1000&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:36:02 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="record-data-source-data">Record data source data</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d__write</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/tree/master/rpc#recordbatch">data</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned if the data is recorded to data source successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission record data to the data source.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/ad75f5b356907f0d2ec7a67d31254410526ef032/data&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;[[1420041600,&quot;1000&quot;]]&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Thu, 08 Jan 2015 11:57:06 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="append-data-source-data-in-json-format">Append data source data in JSON format</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/json</code></p> <p>Write json data</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d__write</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th>Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>safe</code></td> <td>Safe write, server will wait for 1s and scan the data again for safety.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>data-sources/{data-source-rid}/json?safe</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a valid JSON.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned if the JSON data is appended to data source successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission append JSON data to the data source.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if <code>safe</code> is passed in querystring, and fail to append JSON data.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/json&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;how&quot;:&quot;are&quot;,&quot;you&quot;:&quot;?&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:46:49 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="delete-data-source-data">Delete data source data</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/data-sources/{data-source-rid}/data</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the data sources.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <p>This API deletes data points from a data source. The following parameters specify which points to delete:</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>starttime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the start time of window to delete.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?starttime=1416278080</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>endtime</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Unix timestamps that specify the end time of window to delete.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?endtime=1416278417</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>sort</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Defines how to order the points before applying <code>&quot;limit&quot;</code>. This affects which points are deleted in the case where there are more than <code>&quot;limit&quot;</code> points in the specified time window.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?sort=desc</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Sets the maximum number of data points to delete. When set to <code>&quot;infinity&quot;</code> it will delete all the data points in the given window.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/data-sources/[{data-source-rid},{data-source-rid},...]/data?limit=2</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>For more details about these options, see <a href="#get-data-source-data">Get data source data</a>.</p> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the data source is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete the data source.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the data sources rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Delete data without options</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/data&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Tue, 13 Jan 2015 04:40:50 GMT Status: 204 No Content Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><ul> <li>Delete data with options</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/data-sources/4f39859d41a66468cf1e5e28d08ad2cab45b498f/data?starttime=1416278080&amp;endtime=1416278417&amp;limit=2&amp;sort=desc&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Tue, 13 Jan 2015 04:40:50 GMT Status: 204 No Content Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h3 id="device">Device</h3> <h4 id="create-new-device-under-a-portal-of-authenticated-user">Create new device under a portal of authenticated user</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/device</code></p> <p>Creates a new device based on a client model, returning the CIK and RID of the new device.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p_manage</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Requires authentication.</li> <li><p>The following keys are passed:</p> <ul> <li><p><code>&quot;portal_rid&quot;</code> - resource ID of portal where the device is to be created. User creating the device must have at least manager level access to this portal. This may be found in the output of the /portal/ API call, or in Portals here: https://<subdomain>.exosite.com/admin/portallist</p> <p><img src="images/find_portal_rid.png" alt="Find Portal RID"></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;vendor&quot;</code> - vendor identifier. Administrators may find this identifier here: https://<subdomain>.exosite.com/admin/home</p> <p><img src="images/find_vendor.png" alt="Find Vendor ID"></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;model&quot;</code> - client model of device to create. Administrators may find this here, at the bottom of the page: https://<subdomain>.exosite.com/admin/managemodels</p> <p><img src="images/find_model.png" alt="Find Model"></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;serialnumber&quot;</code> - serial number of new device. The serial numbers available are configurable per device model. Administrators may configure individual serial numbers, or configure a range, here: https://<subdomain>.exosite.com/admin/serialnumbers For example, this model has serial numbers consisting of six base 10 digits, e.g. 123456.</p> <p><img src="images/find_serialnumber.png" alt="Find device serial number"></p> </li> <li><p><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - device name. This is a human-readable name for the device.</p> </li> <li><code>&quot;timezone&quot;</code> - device timezone (optional)</li> <li><p><code>&quot;location&quot;</code> - device location (optional)</p> <p>The domain name in the HTTP request indicates which domain to authenticate the user, and must be the same domain in which portal_rid is registered.</p> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><p><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if device is created successful, and along with a JSON object contains following keys:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;rid&quot;</code> - resource identifier for created device</li> <li><p><code>&quot;cik&quot;</code> - key for created device</p> <p>After creating a device, it is necessary to activate it using the provisioning API. This is normally done by device firmware, but may also be done at the command line for testing. [<a href="https://github.com/exosite/api/blob/master/provision/device.md#provisionactivate">https://github.com/exosite/api/blob/master/provision/device.md#provisionactivate</a>] The RID and CIK may then be used with Exosite’s other APIs to interact with the device.</p> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned along body contains a JSON formatted response object. The response object may contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;errors&quot;</code> - array of error identifier strings<ul> <li><code>&quot;limit&quot;</code> - portal’s device limit has been reached</li> <li><code>&quot;invalid_sn&quot;</code> - serial number is invalid</li> <li><code>&quot;unavailable_sn&quot;</code> - serial number is not available</li> <li><code>&quot;forbidden_model&quot;</code> - model is not available in this domain (this also results if <code>&quot;vendor&quot;</code> is invalid or otherwise does not correspond to <code>&quot;model&quot;</code>)</li> <li><code>&quot;require_purchase&quot;</code> - creating this type of device requires a purchase</li> <li><code>&quot;insufficient_resources&quot;</code> - device could not be added due to insufficient resources in the portal</li> <li><code>&quot;portal_not_found&quot;</code> - portal_rid could not be found</li> <li><code>&quot;missing_*&quot;</code> - some required input was missing. E.g. <code>missing_portal_rid</code> indicates missing or empty (blank) portal_rid.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;notices&quot;</code> - array of user-readable error strings</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create the device.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Create the device:</li> </ul> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/device&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;model&quot;: &quot;myDeviceModel&quot;, &quot;vendor&quot;:&quot;joevendor&quot;, &quot;serialnumber&quot;:&quot;ABC-123&quot;, &quot;location&quot;:&quot;Samoa&quot;, &quot;timezone&quot;:&quot;(GMT-11:00) Midway Island, Samoa&quot;, &quot;portal_rid&quot;: &quot;5ef46b987385aaaaaaaaaa75183fb43edeb3557b&quot;, &quot;name&quot;:&quot;Device Name&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 01:45:37 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 99 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;1767af3da6283354eb4818a709db4a0c15756eel&quot;, &quot;cik&quot;: &quot;a148dd4b498cf18c8f1b066af0dab8d671a79a5l&quot; } </code></pre><ul> <li>Then activate the device. Normally this would be done from the device firmware, but we do it here from the command line as an example.</li> </ul> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://m2.exosite.com/provision/activate&#39; \ -d &#39;vendor=joevendor&amp;model=myDeviceModel&amp;sn=ABC-123&#39; </code></pre><pre><code>a148dd4b498cf18c8f1b066af0dab8d671a79a5l </code></pre><h3 id="devices">Devices</h3> <h4 id="create-device">Create device</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}/devices</code></p> <p>Create a device inside a portal</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p_m_crea</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#device-object">device object</a>. Currently only the following keys are supported:</p> <ul> <li><p><code>&quot;type&quot;</code> - Device type, could be either <code>generic</code> or <code>vendor</code> (required)</p> <p>If <code>&quot;type&quot;</code> is <code>vendor</code>, the following keys are required:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;model&quot;</code> - Model name (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;sn&quot;</code> - Serial number (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;vendor&quot;</code> - Vendor name (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if the device is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the portalid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <p>Generic type</p> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/1284862590/devices&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;generic&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 28 Apr 2015 11:11:56 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 877 Content-Type: application/json; } </code></pre><h4 id="update-device">Update device</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/devices/{device-rid}</code></p> <p>Update a device</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_update</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the device.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#device-object">device object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;info&quot;: {&quot;description&quot;: ...}</code> - description under info (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if the device is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/devices/5d4bacb783b10600e12b759bb1ae80b43666085b&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;: {&quot;description&quot;: {&quot;name&quot;: &quot;device update name&quot;}}}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:22:12 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 780 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;dataSources&quot;: [], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;aliases&quot;: [], &quot;basic&quot;: { &quot;modified&quot;: 1416277250, &quot;subscribers&quot;: 0, &quot;type&quot;: &quot;client&quot;, &quot;status&quot;: &quot;activated&quot; }, &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;limits&quot;: { &quot;client&quot;: 0, &quot;dataport&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;datarule&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;disk&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;dispatch&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;email&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;email_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;http&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;http_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;share&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;sms&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;sms_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;xmpp&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;xmpp_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot; Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;info&quot;: {&quot;description&quot;: ...}</code> - description under info (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an object <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if the device is updated successfully. However if any devices fails to update it would still return 200 OK along with an error object included in the response body. (see error exmaple)</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/devices/\[d13da92f1f73f9c5dcf14ef4ce7f43636c277fa6,b2618de3b54cab517a3a347e1cba5a014ae26d62\]&#39; If you want to get more than one device information can reference <a href="#get-multiple-devices">Get multiple devices</a>.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d___view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the device.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if caller user has permission to get the device.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/devices/5d4bacb783b10600e12b759bb1ae80b43666085b&#39;\ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:19:42 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 776 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;dataSources&quot;: [], &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;aliases&quot;: [], &quot;basic&quot;: { &quot;modified&quot;: 1416213844, &quot;subscribers&quot;: 0, &quot;type&quot;: &quot;client&quot;, &quot;status&quot;: &quot;activated&quot; This also resets the status of the associated serial number.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_update</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the device.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the device is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete the device.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/devices/5d4bacb783b10600e12b759bb1ae80b43666085b&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 07:45:09 GMT Status: 204 No Content Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h3 id="domain">Domain</h3> <h4 id="list-domains-of-authenticated-user">List domains of authenticated user</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/domain/</code></p> <p>Returns an array of domains to which the user’s account is added.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User can get information of the domain that the user is a member of.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if get domain information successfully, and along with an array of domain objects. Domain objects contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;rid&quot;</code> - domain rid.</li> <li><code>&quot;domain&quot;</code> - the domain address. This may be used in a subsequent call to /api/portals/v1/portal/</li> <li><code>&quot;role&quot;</code> - the user’s role on this domain. Has one of the following values:<ul> <li><code>&quot;user&quot;</code> - non-admin.</li> <li><code>&quot;admin&quot;</code> - domain admin. If user <code>&quot;role&quot;</code> is <code>&quot;user&quot;</code>, that domain objects will not contain the following keys:</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - vendor name (for provisioning API)</li> <li><code>&quot;token&quot;</code> - vendor token (for provisioning API)</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/domain&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:54:40 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;role&quot;:&quot;user&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;3fd70884cd1e406cd45a7eac898de5d2e6d20d12&quot;, &quot;domain&quot;:&quot;portals.exosite.com&quot; }, { &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;3fd70884cd1e406cd45a7eac898de5d2e6d20d11&quot; &quot;role&quot;:&quot;admin&quot;, &quot;domain&quot;:&quot;joesdomain.exosite.com&quot;, &quot;name&quot;:&quot;joesdomain&quot;, &quot;token&quot;:&quot;01233fb43edeb3557b5ef46b987385abcdef0123&quot; } ] </code></pre><h3 id="domain-widgets">Domain Widgets</h3> <h4 id="create-domain-widget">Create domain widget</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/widget-scripts</code></p> <p>Create a domain widget.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a>.</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;code&quot;</code> - Domain widget code (optional).</li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> - Domain widget description (optional).</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - Domain widget name (required).</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a> if the domain widget is created successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create the domain widget.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;code&quot;:&quot;function(){}&quot;,&quot;description&quot;:&quot;no operation&quot;,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;noop&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Thu, 02 Apr 2015 18:14:40 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 84 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;code&quot;: &quot;function(){}&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;no operation&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3396985491&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;noop&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="delete-domain-widget">Delete domain widget</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</code></p> <p>Delete a domain widget.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the domain widget is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete the domain widget.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the widget script id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/3396985491&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Thu, 02 Apr 2015 18:59:11 GMT Status: 204 No Content Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="get-domain-widget">Get domain widget</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</code></p> <p>Get a domain widget.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a> if the caller user has permission to get domain widget.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get the domain widget.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the widget script id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/3396985491&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Thu, 02 Apr 2015 18:18:28 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 84 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;code&quot;: &quot;function(){}&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;no operation&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3396985491&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;noop&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="list-domain-widget">List domain widget</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/widget-scripts</code></p> <p>List domain widget.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a> if the caller user has permission to get domain widget.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get the domain widget.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Thu, 02 Apr 2015 18:24:58 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 86 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;code&quot;: &quot;function(){}&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;no operation&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3396985491&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;noop&quot; } ] </code></pre><h4 id="update-domain-widget">Update domain widget</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/{widget-script-id}</code></p> <p>Update a domain widget.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a>.</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;code&quot;</code> - Domain widget code (optional).</li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> - Domain widget description (optional).</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - Domain widget name (optional).</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#domain-widget-object">domain widget object</a> if the domain widget is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the domain widget.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the widget script id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/widget-scripts/3396985491&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;code&quot;:&quot;&quot;},&quot;description&quot;:&quot;empty&quot;,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;empty&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Thu, 02 Apr 2015 18:58:01 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 66 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;code&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;empty&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3396985491&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;empty&quot; } </code></pre><h3 id="file-systems">File Systems</h3> <pre><code>&lt;form action=&quot;/api/portals/v1/fs/{directory-path}&quot; enctype=&quot;multipart/form-data&quot; method=&quot;POST&quot;&gt; &lt;div&gt; &lt;input name=&quot;{field-name-1}&quot; type=&quot;file&quot;&gt; &lt;input name=&quot;{field-name-2}&quot; type=&quot;text&quot;&gt; &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;Submit&lt;/button&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/form&gt; </code></pre><ul> <li><code>&lt;directory-path&gt;</code> can be <code>[\/\-_0-9A-Za-z]*</code>.</li> <li><code>&lt;field-name-*&gt;</code> is <code>^[\-0-9_A-Za-z]*$</code>.</li> </ul> <p>Submission of this form redirects the page to &quot;/api/portals/v1/fs/{directory-path}/{subdirectory}&quot;.</p> <p>The response entity body is:</p> <pre><code>{ {field-name-1}: {field-content-type-1}, {field-name-2}: {field-value-2} } </code></pre><ul> <li><code>{field-name-*}</code> is the literal send in the request.</li> <li><code>{field-content-type-1}</code> is the content type of the file as the value of field 1.</li> <li><code>{field-value-2}</code> is the value of <code>{field-name-2}</code>.</li> </ul> <p>The file system sets the Content-Type of a GET response according to its file extension. Supported file extensions are:</p> <p>ai, bmp, cab, css, doc, eps, exe, flv, gif, htm, html, ico, jpe, jpeg, jpg, js, json, mov, mp3, msi, ods, odt, pdf, php, png, ppt, ps, psd, qt, rar, rtf, svg, svgz, swf, tif, tiff, txt, xls, xml, zip.</p> <h4 id="append-to-a-directory">Append to a directory</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/fs</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_____fs</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body must not be empty</li> <li>Request header must contain <code>Content-Type</code></li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>303 See Other</code>: Returned along with the file content if the file is appended successfully, the field directory will appear in <code>Location</code>.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to append the file.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>500 Internal Server Error</code>: Returned if request header doesn&#39;t contain <code>Content-Type</code>.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs&#39; \ -X POST \ -H &#39;Content-Type: application/json&#39; \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hello&quot;}}]}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 303 See Other Date: Tue, 16 Jun 2015 01:43:31 GMT Status: 303 See Other Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/141517041216756400 Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 43 Content-Type: application/json {&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hello&quot;}}]} </code></pre><h4 id="list-files">List files</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/fs</code></p> <p>Get all files which under the same directory.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to get file content.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a JSON entity.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example-without-file-extension">Example without file extension</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Wed, 19 Nov 2014 09:09:03 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 21 Content-Type: application/json { &quot;143442117468881900&quot;: { &quot;info&quot;: [ { &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;name&quot;: &quot;hello1&quot; } } ] }, &quot;143442118299661000&quot;: { &quot;info&quot;: [ { &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;name&quot;: &quot;hello2&quot; } } ] } } </code></pre><h5 id="example-with-file-extension">Example with file extension</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs.js&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Wed, 19 Nov 2014 09:09:03 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 21 Content-Type: application/javascript console.log(&quot;Hello JavaScript&quot;); </code></pre><h4 id="get-a-file">Get a file</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/fs/{directory-path}/{subdirectory}</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to get a file.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned with a body containing the object previously uploaded by the user.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the directory of field is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>IF the myfile is a image file:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/path/141517041216756400&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:41:13 GMT Status: 200 OK Content-Length: 82 Content-Type: image/png {&quot;myfile&quot;:&quot;image\/png; @md5=a6cfdf1c6d7fb1574a66fd06a94f4435&quot;} </code></pre><h4 id="get-file-content">Get file content</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/fs/{directory-path}/{subdirectory}/{field-name}</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to get file content.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned with a body containing the object previously uploaded by the user.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the directory of field is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>IF the myfile is a image file:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/path/141517041216756400/myfile&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:41:13 GMT Status: 200 OK Content-Length: 82 Content-Type: image/png ▒PNG IHDR%▒V▒PLTEA▒▒▒▒V▒ IDATx▒cb67|▒IEND▒B`▒ </code></pre><ul> <li>IF the myfile is a text file:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/path/141517041216756401/myfile&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 06:58:14 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 43 Content-Type: application/json {&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hello&quot;}}]} </code></pre><h4 id="update-file-content">Update file content</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/fs/{directory-path}</code></p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_____fs</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body must not be empty</li> <li>Request header must contain <code>Content-Type</code>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing file content if the file is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with file content and file directory appear in <code>Location</code> if the file directory does not exist.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the file.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>500 Internal Server Error</code>: Returned if request header doesn&#39;t contain <code>Content-Type</code>.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>IF the file directory exist:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/aa&#39; \ -X PUT \ -H &#39;Content-Type: application/json&#39; \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hell2&quot;}}]}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 23 Jun 2015 08:06:23 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 43 Content-Type: application/json {&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hell2&quot;}}]} </code></pre><ul> <li>IF the file directory does not exist:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/aa&#39; \ -X PUT \ -H &#39;Content-Type: application/json&#39; \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hell1&quot;}}]}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 23 Jun 2015 07:25:00 GMT Status: 201 Created Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/fs/aa Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 43 Content-Type: application/json {&quot;info&quot;:[{&quot;description&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;hell1&quot;}}]} </code></pre><h3 id="groups">Groups</h3> <h4 id="create-group-under-user">Create group under user</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/groups</code></p> <p>Create a group under a user. A group under a user may be updated only by that user. (TODO: confirm this)</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can create a group under himself.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_s_crea</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>The request body is a <a href="#group-object">group object</a>. Currently, only the following keys are supported:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - group name (optional) If you send keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#group-object">group object</a> if the group is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the directory of field is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if the group name exists already.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/groups&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;new group&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:48:23 GMT Status: 201 Created Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/1206252898 Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 163 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;id&quot;: &quot;1206252898&quot;, &quot;userId&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;members&quot;: [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;User&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot; } } ], &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;new group&quot;, &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h4 id="update-group">Update group</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/groups/{group-id}</code></p> <p>Update a group</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>g_update</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the group.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>force</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The update group permission will now ignore all bad and non existing permissions.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/{group-id}?force=true</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Body contains a <a href="#group-object">group object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;members&quot;</code> - group members (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;meta&quot;</code> - group meta (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - group name (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;permissions&quot;</code> - group permissions (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#group-object">group object</a> if the group is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the group id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/1206252898&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;update group name&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:52:44 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 171 Content-Type: application/json; } } ], &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;update group name&quot;, &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h4 id="get-group">Get group</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/groups/{group-id}</code></p> <p>Get information about a group.</p> <p>If you want to get more than one group information can reference <a href="#get-multiple-groups">Get multiple groups</a>.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>g_member</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the group.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#group-object">group object</a> if caller user has permission to get the group.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the group id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/1206252898&#39; } } ], &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;new group&quot;, &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h4 id="get-group-permissions">Get group permissions</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/groups/{group-id}/permissions</code></p> <p>Get permissions about a group.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>g_member</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the group.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>type</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">An array of permission types to retrieve. The supported types are <code>Domain</code>, <code>Portal</code>, <code>Device</code>, <code>DataSource</code> and <code>Group</code>.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/groups/{group-id}/permissions?type%5B%5D=Group</code> <br> (Square brackets &quot;[&quot; and &quot;]&quot; have been replaced with &quot;%5B&quot; and &quot;%5D&quot; respectively)</td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Number of items to skip, only available when <code>&quot;limit&quot;</code> is valid.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/groups/{group-id}/permissions?offset=0</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Use with limit to paginate the permissions lists.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/groups/{group-id}/permissions?limit=10</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> if the caller user has permission to get the group.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the group id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/1206252898/permissions&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:51:19 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 163 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Device&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &lt;device-rid&gt; } } ] </code></pre><h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/1206252898/permissions?offset=0&amp;limit=1&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:51:19 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 163 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Device&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &lt;device-rid&gt; } } ] </code></pre><h4 id="delete-group">Delete group</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/groups/{group-id}</code></p> <p>Delete a group</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the group.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the group is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete the group.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>500 Internal Server Error</code>: Returned if the group id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/groups/3065555968&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 07:42:00 GMT Status: 204 No Content Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h3 id="portal">Portal</h3> <h4 id="list-portals-of-authenticated-user">List portals of authenticated user</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/portal/</code></p> <p>Get an array of portals for the specified user on the domain specified in the URL of the request.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must be authenticated in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty. The domain name in the HTTP request is used to indicate which domain’s portals should be listed.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the caller user has permission to list portal, and along with a JSON array of portal objects. Portal objects contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - Portal name</li> <li><code>&quot;domain&quot;</code> - Portal domain</li> <li><code>&quot;key&quot;</code> - Portal CIK (returned only if user has &quot;owner&quot; or &quot;manager&quot; level access to the portal)</li> <li><code>&quot;rid&quot;</code> - Portal resource ID</li> <li><code>&quot;role&quot;</code> - User’s role for this portal. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;owner&quot;</code> - user is the portal’s direct owner</li> <li><code>&quot;manager&quot;</code> - user has manager access to the portal. This role grants the same rights as owner. A role of <code>&quot;manager&quot;</code> indicates the portal is not a child client of this user in the One Platform hierarchy. Once you have a key to the portal the distinction is not important to the API, though.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portal&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:45:50 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 1442 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;name&quot;: &quot;Test Sighoff 2014-06-19 16:47:21&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;845e50e84fae7fe3d680f56ab79c7db31e7ab9b3&quot;, &quot;key&quot;: &quot;18279f186f23aea867eaadc1e2af4010017e1dba&quot;, &quot;role&quot;: &quot;owner&quot;, &quot;domain&quot;: &quot;mydomain.exosite.com&quot; }, { &quot;name&quot;: &quot;Test Sighoff 2014-06-19 16:47:21&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;9dd0f4bf2e3a55553cfae85e3b61dcae178e0544&quot;, &quot;key&quot;: &quot;5fbf1cd65803a8b2eeb823eeaf4a92b0bf5f2bd2&quot;, &quot;role&quot;: &quot;owner&quot;, &quot;domain&quot;: &quot;mydomain.exosite.com&quot; }, ... ] </code></pre><h3 id="portals">Portals</h3> <h4 id="create-portal">Create portal</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/portals</code></p> <p>Create a portal under a user. The created portal will have the same device, data sources, events, alerts and scripts as the Default Portal Template in /admin/portaltemplate if Default Portal Template is not &quot;no template&quot;.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_p_crea</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#portal-object">portal object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be included:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;planId&quot;</code> - portals plan ID from signup page, e.g. <a href="https://portals.exosite.com/signup?plan=3676938388">https://portals.exosite.com/signup?plan=3676938388</a>. Plan must allow free signups.(optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#portal-object">portal object</a> if the portal is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create the portal.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;planId&quot;:&quot;3676938388&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:52:58 GMT Status: 201 Created Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/3882920427 Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 578 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;devices&quot;: [ &quot;3fb37448bc68d4c84d58c755fd29f187edc74694&quot; ], &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3882920427&quot;, &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;aliases&quot;: [], &quot;basic&quot;: { &quot;modified&quot;: 1416217920, &quot;subscribers&quot;: 0, &quot;type&quot;: &quot;client&quot;, &quot;status&quot;: &quot;activated&quot; }, &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;limits&quot;: { &quot;client&quot;: 5, &quot;dataport&quot;: 50, &quot;datarule&quot;: 50, &quot;disk&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;dispatch&quot;: 50, &quot;email&quot;: 10, &quot;email_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;http&quot;: 100, &quot;http_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;share&quot;: 100, &quot;sms&quot;: 10, &quot;sms_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot;, &quot;xmpp&quot;: 100, &quot;xmpp_bucket&quot;: &quot;inherit&quot; }, &quot;locked&quot;: false, &quot;meta&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;name&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;public&quot;: false }, &quot;key&quot;: &quot;9ebc9f396e86995fe52cc77a9533675c0ac8876d&quot;, &quot;shares&quot;: [], &quot;subscribers&quot;: [], &quot;tagged&quot;: [], &quot;tags&quot;: [] } } </code></pre><h4 id="update-portal">Update portal</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}</code></p> <p>Update information about a portal.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p_manage</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#portal-object">portal object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;info&quot;</code> - Info is an object. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;aliases&quot;</code> - Aliases under info is an array.(optional) Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>{rid}</code> - The under this portal&#39;s data-sources/ device rid. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;{aliases}&quot;</code> - The under this portal&#39;s data-sources/ device aliases is an array.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> - Description under info (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#portal-object">portal object</a> if the portal is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update the portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/3882920427&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;info&quot;:{&quot;aliases&quot;:{&quot;3fb37448bc68d4c84d58c755fd29f187edc74694&quot;:[&quot;update aliases&quot;]}}}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 10:03:21 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding portal</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}</code></p> <p>Get information about a portal.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p___view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> /api/portals/v1/portals</code></p> <p>List portal by domain.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_p_list</code> <a id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of portal id if caller user has permission to list portal.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 </code></pre><h4 id="list-portal-device">List portal device</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-id}/devices</code></p> <p>List portal device.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>p___view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Number of items to limit</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/portals/{portal-id}/devices?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#device-object">device object</a> if caller user has permission to list portal device.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must be authenticated in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the portal is deleted successfully.</li> <li>Returned if failed to delete portal due to device under that portal is being used as a Clone for other devices.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/1156616498&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u application/json; charset=UTF-8 [&quot;myportal has been successfully deleted.&quot;] </code></pre><h4 id="delete-portal-by-rid">Delete portal by RID</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/portals/{portal-rid}/ByRid</code></p> <p>Delete a portal through portal ID.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must be authenticated in the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the portal is deleted successfully.</li> <li>Returned if failed to delete portal due to device under that portal is being used as a Clone for other devices.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the portal rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/portals/de3d88a4c15a341d386e7c1cfa0fa2a3a4cf2dcb/ByRid&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Wed, 19 Nov 2014 01:59:13 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 52 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [&quot;myportal has been successfully deleted.&quot;] </code></pre><h3 id="scripts">Scripts</h3> <h4 id="create-device-script">Create device script</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/devices/{device-rid}/scripts</code></p> <p>Create a device script.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_update</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the device.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <pre><code>{ &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;description&quot;: { &quot;name&quot;: string = &quot;&quot;, &quot;rule&quot;: { &quot;script&quot;: string = &quot;&quot; } } } } </code></pre><ul> <li>See <a href="https://github.com/exosite/docs/blob/master/rpc/README.md#create-datarule">create datarule API</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#script-object">script object</a> if the device script is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create device script.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get device script.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the device rid is id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the portal.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <pre><code>{ &quot;info&quot;: { &quot;description&quot;: &lt;description&gt; } } </code></pre><ul> <li><p><code>&lt;description&gt;</code> - See <a <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update script.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the script rid is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/scripts/28571049e6bf6de245012957171da9e83926d897&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d domain. Only a domain administrator user can use these Theme APIs. All theme APIs share the same prefix: <code>/api/portals/v1/themes/</code>. <strong>Note: Image data can currently not be modified using this API</strong></p> <h4 id="create-theme">Create theme</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/themes</code></p> <p>Create default theme the exosite system theme will be applied to the domain.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have <code>___admin</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Body contains a <a href="#theme-object">theme object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;name&quot;</code> - theme name (required)</li> <li><code>&quot;description&quot;</code> - theme permissions (required) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#theme-object">theme object</a> if the theme is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to create theme.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/themes&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;name&quot;:&quot;test1113&quot;,&quot;description&quot;:&quot;desc-test1113&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Mon, 27 Apr 2015 08:15:57 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Type: application/json;
