charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h3 id="user">User</h3> <h4 id="register-new-user-account">Register new user account</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/user</code></p> <blockquote> <p><strong>Deprecated.</strong> This API is deprecated and should not be used.</p> </blockquote> <p>Signs up a new user account, sending an activation email to the specified address.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to create a new user.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a JSON object with the following keys:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - new user’s email address (required)</li> <li><code>&quot;password&quot;</code> - new user’s password (required)</li> <li><code>&quot;plan&quot;</code> - portals plan ID from signup page, e.g. <a href="https://portals.exosite.com/signup?plan=3676938388">https://portals.exosite.com/signup?plan=3676938388</a>. Plan must allow free signups. (required)</li> <li><code>&quot;first_name&quot;</code> - user’s first name (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;last_name&quot;</code> - user’s last name (optional) If <code>&quot;first_name&quot;</code> or <code>&quot;last_name&quot;</code> are omitted or empty, they are set to <code>&quot;New&quot;</code> and <code>&quot;User&quot;</code>, respectively.</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>The domain name in the HTTP request is used to indicate which domain the user should be signed up in.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the user is created successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned along with JSON formatted response object. Response object may contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;errors&quot;</code> - array of error identifier strings.<ul> <li><code>&quot;missing_*&quot;</code> - some required input was missing. E.g. missing_email indicates missing or empty (blank) email.</li> <li><code>&quot;wrong_password&quot;</code> - email is already registered with Portals and the password is incorrect.</li> <li><code>&quot;user_exists_wrong_domain”</code> - user exists on another domain.</li> <li><code>&quot;user_exists&quot;</code> - user already exists on this domain.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;notices&quot;</code> - array of user-readable error strings.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/user&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;jane+testuser123@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;password&quot;:&quot;testuserP4ssword&quot;, &quot;plan&quot;:&quot;3676938388&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 06:24:51 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: text/html </code></pre><h4 id="reset-user-account-password">Reset user account password</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/user/password</code></p> <blockquote> <p><strong>Deprecated.</strong> This API is deprecated and should not be used.</p> </blockquote> <p>Sends a password reset email for this user.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to reset password.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request contains a JSON object with the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - email address of a Portals user.</li> <li><code>&quot;action&quot;</code> - what to do. Supported values:<ul> <li><code>&quot;reset&quot;</code> - send user a password reset request</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if reset password request is allowed, will receive a reset password email.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned along with JSON formatted response object. Response object may contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;errors&quot;</code> - array of error identifier strings.<ul> <li><code>&quot;missing_*&quot;</code> - some required input was missing. E.g. missing_email indicates missing or empty (blank) email.</li> <li><code>&quot;failed&quot;</code> - some other error occurred.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;notices&quot;</code> - array of user-readable error strings.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>$ curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/user/password&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;reset&quot;, &quot;email&quot;: &quot;joe@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:16:12 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: text/html </code></pre><h3 id="users">Users</h3> <h4 id="create-user">Create user</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users</code></p> <p>Create a user.</p> <ul> <li>Non-admin and admin users can create a new account</li> <li>To create a new user, Moderate New User Signup must be set to <strong>OFF</strong> from admin/moderate page.</li> <li>Depending on the request, an activation email may be sent to the user<ul> <li>To send an activation email, include the <code>X-User-Agent</code> header. This also requires some extra configuration. A default plan for <strong>Automatically create a portal for any user who signs up from another domain</strong> from admin/configuration page. <img src="images/find_default_portal_setting.png" alt="Find Default Portal Setting"></li> <li>To not send an activation email, omit the <code>X-User-Agent</code> header.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to create a new user.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a <a href="#user-object">user object</a>. Currently only the following keys may be included:<ul> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - User email. (required)</li> <li><code>&quot;userName&quot;</code> - User name. (optional) If it has no this attribute then userName will be same as email.</li> <li><code>&quot;password&quot;</code> - User password. (optional) If omitted, a random password is created.</li> <li><code>&quot;Firstname&quot;</code> - User first name. (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;Lastname&quot;</code> - User last name. (optional) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <p>If it has Firstname and Lastname then the fullName in your response body will be Firstname + Lastname.</p> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the new user is created successfully, and will receive an email with a randomly generated password.</li> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned if creating user with header containing X-User-Agent and the new user is created successfully, will receive an activation email.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the email has already registered and is awaiting activation.</li> <li>Returned if the email already has an account in this domain.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Creating user with header containing X-User-Agent.</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users&#39; \ -X POST \ -H &#39;X-User-Agent: Android&#39; \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted Date: Thu, 05 Feb 2015 04:02:27 GMT Status: 202 Accepted Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 184 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;code&quot;: 202, &quot;message&quot;: &quot;Thank you. You will receive an email confirming your new account shortly. That email will contain a link to validate and complete the account creation process.&quot; } </code></pre><ul> <li>Creating user with header not containing X-User-Agent.</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:12:25 GMT Status: 201 Created Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h4 id="activate-a-user-account-using-activation-key">Activate a user account using activation key</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users</code></p> <p>Activate an activation email.</p> <ul> <li>The activation email is created by POST /users to create the user with header contains X-User-Agent</li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to activate an activation email.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a JSON object. Currently only the following key may be included:<ul> <li><code>&quot;activationRegkey&quot;</code> - activation key (required)(Activation key can be found in the activation email that was sent when creating a user by making POST request to /users endpoint with header containing X-User-Agent.) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the new user is activated successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the activation key not existing this domain.</li> <li>Returned if request body is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;activationRegkey&quot;:&quot;21c2bdc303c23f5841b35fd0935efca42803fdeb&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 10 Mar 2015 06:31:25 GMT Vary: Accept-Encoding Cache-Control: max-age=0, no-cache Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: text/html </code></pre><h4 id="update-user">Update user</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}</code></p> <p>Update a Portals user information.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can update his own account information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_list</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>silence</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The <a href="#user-object">user object</a> will not be returned in the response body.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/{user-id}?silence</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request body is a <a href="#user-object">user object</a>. At the moment, only the following keys may be updated:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;activated&quot;</code> - Whether a user is activated (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - User email. (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;userName&quot;</code> - User name.(optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;fullName&quot;</code> - User full name. (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;password&quot;</code> - User password.(optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;meta&quot;</code> -User meta. (optional)</li> <li><code>&quot;permissions&quot;</code> - User permissions. (optional)</li> <li><p><code>&quot;phoneNumber&quot;</code> - user phone number. (optional)</p> <p>If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</p> <p>When User-A update User-B, User-A doesn&#39;t need to grant permission of resources from User-B which User-A doesn&#39;t have.</p> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the callee user is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned if <code>silence</code> is passed in querystring, and the callee user is updated successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to update user.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;updatedemail@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:33:44 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;updatedemail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h5 id="example-with-options">Example with options</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736?silence&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;updatedemail@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:33:44 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 0 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="reset-password">Reset password</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/reset-password</code></p> <p>Step 1 of 2: Send a reset password email to user account.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to reset password.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a JSON object. Currently only the following key may be included:<ul> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - User email (required) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned along with a body containing a message if reset password allowed, will receive a reset password email.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the email address has not registered.</li> <li>Returned if request body is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/reset-password&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;resetEmail@gmail.com&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted Date: Tue, 17 Mar 2015 04:06:36 GMT Status: 202 Accepted Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 187 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;code&quot;:202, &quot;message&quot;:&quot;Thank you. We have sent an email to your account&#39;s registered email address. The email contains a link that will allow you to complete the password reset process.&quot; } </code></pre><h4 id="reset-user-profile-picture">Reset user profile picture</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/profile/picture</code></p> <p>Reset user profile picture to default.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can update his own account information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned if the user profile picture is reset successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to reset callee user profile picture.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/profile/picture&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 06:20:40 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 </code></pre><h4 id="set-user-profile-picture">Set user profile picture</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/profile/picture</code></p> <p>Set user profile picture by uploading file.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can set his profile picture.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is the file user intends to upload and only supports png image file.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned if the user profile picture is uploaded successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to upload callee user&#39;s profile picture.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/profile/picture&#39; \ -X POST \ -F myfile=@&quot;~/Downloads/user1-64x64.png&quot; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 100 Continue HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 06:30:51 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 </code></pre><h4 id="update-password-by-reset-password-key">Update password by reset password key</h4> <p><code>PUT /api/portals/v1/users/reset-password</code></p> <p>Step 2 of 2: Activate a reset password email.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Anyone can use this endpoint to reset password.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is a JSON object. Currently only the following keys may be included:<ul> <li><code>&quot;resetPasswordRegkey&quot;</code> - Reset key (required) (Reset key can be found in the reset email that was sent upon POST request to /users/reset-password with the email address)</li> <li><code>&quot;newPassword&quot;</code> - User new password (optional) (A random password will be generated if <code>&quot;newPassword&quot;</code> option is not specified) If you send any keys besides these, it will do nothing.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the user password is reset successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/reset-password&#39; \ -X PUT \ -d &#39;{&quot;resetPasswordRegkey&quot;:&quot;21c2bdc303c23f5841b35fd0935efca42803fdeb&quot;, &quot;newPassword&quot;:&quot;newPassword&quot;}&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Tue, 17 Mar 2015 04:09:36 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 113 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="get-all-users">Get all users</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users</code></p> <p>Get information about all users.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>offset</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">Use with limit to pagenation the user lists.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users?offset=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>limit</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">see Offset.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users?limit=10</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>NoPermissions</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The <a href="#user-object">user object</a> will not include permission items.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users?NoPermissions</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the caller user has permission to get all users.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get all users.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:21:47 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;: [] }, { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;olduser&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3407735538&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;: [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Domain&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;0000000000&quot; } } ] }, ... ] </code></pre><h5 id="example-with-options">Example with options</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users?offset=0&amp;limit=10&amp;NoPermissions&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:21:47 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], }, { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;existinguseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;olduser&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3407735538&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], }, ... ] </code></pre><h4 id="get-all-user-portals">Get all user portals</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/portals</code></p> <p>Get user&#39;s permission information regarding portals he owns or shared from other users.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own portals information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>options</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">The portal object will include devices item is an array of devices RIDs. The supported option is <code>devices</code>.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>/users/{user-id}/portals?options=devices</code></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if get user portals successfully, will along with an array of portal object. Portal objects contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;PortalName&quot;</code> - Portal name.</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalID&quot;</code> - Portal ID.</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalRID&quot;</code> - Portal RID.</li> <li><code>&quot;UserEmail&quot;</code> - The user&#39;s email.</li> <li><code>&quot;Description&quot;</code> - Portal description.</li> <li><code>&quot;Permissions&quot;</code> - User’s permission for this portal. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;___admin&quot;</code> - user is the portal’s direct owner</li> <li><code>&quot;p_manage&quot;</code> - user has manager access to the portal. This permission grants the same rights as owner.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_m_crea&quot;</code> - user has create device access to the portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_contac&quot;</code> - user has receive alerts access from the portal.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user portals.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 09:36:45 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 339 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;PortalName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;PortalID&quot;: &quot;2853566858&quot;, &quot;PortalRID&quot;: &quot;6800e1ee0948d39744625990d28d360f78ac2e4d&quot;, &quot;UserEmail&quot;: &quot;useremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;Description&quot;: &quot;Default Portal&quot;, &quot;Permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;___admin&quot;}] }, { &quot;PortalName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;PortalID&quot;: &quot;2978406756&quot;, &quot;PortalRID&quot;: &quot;dd6e30fe1a00a9718b919ccd93601ff10310238b&quot;, &quot;UserEmail&quot;: &quot;useremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;Description&quot;: &quot;Default Portal&quot; &quot;Permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;p_manage&quot;} } ... ] </code></pre><h4 id="example-with-options">Example with options</h4> <pre><code>curl https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals?options=devices \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i [ { &quot;PortalName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;PortalID&quot;: &quot;2853566858&quot;, &quot;PortalRID&quot;: &quot;6800e1ee0948d39744625990d28d360f78ac2e4d&quot;, &quot;UserEmail&quot;: &quot;useremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;Description&quot;: &quot;Default Portal&quot;, &quot;Permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;___admin&quot;}] &quot;Devices&quot;:[&quot;acf4838d1aa26e00ae834c1ab67884e21137c1b7&quot;,&quot;c36ec9302b2fa9b43772ba7a72da3e74efb3dc92&quot;] }, { &quot;PortalName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;PortalID&quot;: &quot;2978406756&quot;, &quot;PortalRID&quot;: &quot;dd6e30fe1a00a9718b919ccd93601ff10310238b&quot;, &quot;UserEmail&quot;: &quot;useremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;Description&quot;: &quot;Default Portal&quot; &quot;Permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;p_manage&quot;} &quot;Devices&quot;:[] } ... ] </code></pre><h4 id="get-user">Get user</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}</code></p> <p>Get information about a user.</p> <p>If you want to get more than one user information can refer to <a href="#get-multiple-users">Get multiple users</a>.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own portals information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the caller user has permission to get callee user.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:18:40 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;: &quot;newuseremail@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;: &quot;72ab11cdb1b5025e0f8ae8fe78b1c0c949751090&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;: null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;: &quot;&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;: true, &quot;groups&quot;: [], &quot;permissions&quot;: [] } </code></pre><h3 id="get-user-through-readtoken">Get user through readtoken</h3> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}?readtoken={user-readtoken}</code></p> <p>Get the user information through readtoken.</p> <ul> <li>The token expires in 5 min once its generated.</li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have readtoken.</li> </ul> <h4 id="request">Request</h4> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h4 id="response">Response</h4> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing a <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the caller user has permission to get callee user.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h4 id="example">Example</h4> <pre><code>curl https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736?readtoken=kDRv-JHtAjeECWSineeCRTVM-ZZyVUjpwrWLKc3DFuAjOokBcXrxtHQJ-immZyyRZbco9rG_TuOGqPpx1MRw5cvPgfEO \ -H &#39;Content-Type: application/json&#39; \ -u &#39;domainuseremail@gmail.com:domainuserP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:18:40 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 144 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 { &quot;email&quot;:&quot;doaminUser1@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;fullName&quot;:&quot;doamin User1&quot;, &quot;id&quot;:&quot;3167859736&quot;, &quot;rid&quot;:&quot;fc7830446d5053abd0c212294764bb23bdedf0dd&quot;, &quot;meta&quot;:null, &quot;phoneNumber&quot;:&quot;09123456789&quot;, &quot;userName&quot;:&quot;doaminUser1@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;activated&quot;:true,&quot;groups&quot;:[], &quot;permissions&quot;:[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;___admin&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Portal&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;3349395467&quot;}}] } </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-token">Get user token</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/token</code></p> <p>Get a portals user token. This token can be used for logging into a domain or making API calls.</p> <ul> <li>The token expires in 30 days once its generated.</li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own token.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li><p>Request string.</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;reDirect&quot;</code> - URL when login fail reDirect to where..</li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Request body is empty.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the token is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user token.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Create a token</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/token\?reDirect\=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com.tw%2F&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:39:27 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 16 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 &quot;MzE2Nzg1OTczNq==&quot; </code></pre><ul> <li>To use a token, put the token in the Authorization field like illustrated below, response content is skipped for clarity:</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this&#39; \ -H &#39;Authorization: Token MzE2Nzg1OTczNq==&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 21 Nov 2014 08:00:10 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Transfer-Encoding: chunked Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h3 id="get-user-readtoken">Get user readtoken</h3> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/readtoken</code></p> <p>Get a user access token then other users can get this user information without domain admin permission.</p> <ul> <li>The token expires in 5 min once its generated.</li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own readtoken.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h4 id="request">Request</h4> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h4 id="response">Response</h4> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if the readtoken is created successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get user readtoken.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h4 id="example">Example</h4> <pre><code>curl https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/readtoken \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:39:27 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 &quot;kDRv-JHtAjeECWSineeCRTVM-ZZyVUjpwrWLKc3DFuAjOokBcXrxtHQJ-immZyyRZbco9rG_TuOGqPpx1MRw5cvPgfEO&quot; </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-token-for-openid-user">Get user token for OpenID user</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/_this/token</code></p> <p>Get a portals user token. This token can be used for logging into a domain or making API calls.</p> <ul> <li><p>If the OpenID user is a new user for the domain, will create the account and portal, then grant a token from Exosite.</p> </li> <li><p>If the OpenID user is an existing user for the domain, then grant a token from Exosite.</p> </li> <li><p>A new account will only be created, if settings are as followed:</p> <ul> <li>Moderate New User Signup is set to <strong>OFF</strong> from admin/moderate page.</li> <li>Set a default plan for <strong>Automatically create a portal for any user who signs up from another domain</strong> from admin/configuration page. <img src="images/find_default_portal_setting.png" alt="Find Default Portal Setting"></li> </ul> </li> <li><p>The token expires in 30 days once its generated.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>Only support the OpenID Connect user of Google for App.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request header must include some information for Authorization.<ul> <li>Who is Oauth/OpenID server? (E.g. Google)</li> <li>What is the short-lived authorization code of user from authorization server?</li> </ul> </li> <li>Request body is empty.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#user-object">user object</a> if the new user is created successfully, and will receive an email with a randomly generated password.</li> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned if creating user with header containing X-User-Agent and the new user is created successfully, will receive an activation email.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if Moderate New User Signup is set to <strong>ON</strong> from admin/moderate page.</li> <li>Returned if doesn&#39;t set a default plan for <strong>Automatically create a portal for any user who signs up from another domain</strong> from admin/configuration page.</li> <li>Returned if authorization in the header is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the email has already registered and is awaiting activation.</li> <li>Returned if the email already has an account in this domain.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <ul> <li>Create a token</li> </ul> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/token&#39; \ -H &#39;Authorization: Google 4/S39q1GijhAxDVtx5Dwhh-9kpYBvcVj1IFMFc.4vbo5d2l_AdgKnQAx0j5UqlQI&#39; \ -X GET \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:39:27 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 16 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 &quot;MzE2Nzg1OTczNq==&quot; </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-data-storage">Get user data storage</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/ds/{subdirectory}</code></p> <p>Get user data storage.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own data storage.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_list</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing is dependent upon whatever you set, if get user data storage successful.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get user data storage.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li>Returned if the subdirectory is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:01:46 GMT Content-Type: application/json Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 {&quot;myTest&quot;:&quot;123123&quot;} </code></pre><pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds/apple/456&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:03:54 GMT Content-Type: image/png Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 �PNG :���s���=;�q���t�&#39;�)��x����n�M����63��4�d��]��;wd�oݖ�as������gj����j=��D����Ԅ�KO��_ </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-data-storage-list">Get user data storage list</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/ds/{subdirectory}/*</code></p> <p>Get user data storage of list.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own data storage list.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_list</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of data storage if the caller user has permission to get user data storage list.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get user data storage list.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds/*&#39; \ -X GET \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:15:10 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 [&quot;apple&quot;,&quot;dog&quot;] </code></pre><h4 id="create-user-data-storage">Create user data storage</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/ds/{subdirectory}</code></p> <p>Set a user data storage key.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can set his own data storage list.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_list</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is the value you want to set</li> <li><p>Request header must contain one of following as content type:</p> <ul> <li><code>application/json</code></li> <li><code>text/plain</code></li> <li><code>image/gif</code></li> <li><code>image/jpg</code></li> <li><code>image/png</code></li> <li><code>image/bmp</code></li> <li><code>image/jpeg</code></li> <li><code>application/octet-stream</code></li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>201 Created</code>: Returned if the data storage is created successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if not setting Content-Type.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to set user data storage.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds/dog&#39; \ -X POST \ -H &#39;Content-Type: application/json&#39; \ -d &#39;{&quot;myTest&quot;:&quot;1231443534523&quot;}&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:16:10 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 </code></pre><h5 id="example-for-upload-file">Example for upload file</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds/dog&#39; \ -X POST \ -H &#39;Content-Type: image/png&#39; \ -F myfile=@&quot;/Volumes/exosite/review/public/static/png/bullet_go.png&quot; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 100 Continue HTTP/1.1 201 Created Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:03:31 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 </code></pre><h4 id="delete-user-data-storage">Delete user data storage</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/ds/{subdirectory}</code></p> <p>Delete a user data storage key.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can delete his own data storage list.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_list</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the data storage is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete user data storage.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li>Returned if the subdirectory is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/_this/ds/dog&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 09:33:28 GMT Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-portal">Get user portal</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/portals/{portal-id}</code></p> <p>Get a portal&#39;s information owned by a user</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own portal.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with an array of portal object if the caller has permission to get user&#39;s portals. Portal objects contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;PortalName&quot;</code> - Portal name.</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalID&quot;</code> - Portal ID.</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalRID&quot;</code> - Portal RID.</li> <li><code>&quot;UserEmail&quot;</code> - The user&#39;s email.</li> <li><code>&quot;Description&quot;</code> - Portal description.</li> <li><code>&quot;Permissions&quot;</code> - User’s permission for this portal. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;___admin&quot;</code> - user is the portal’s direct owner</li> <li><code>&quot;p_manage&quot;</code> - user has manager access to this portal. This permission grants the same rights as owner.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_m_crea&quot;</code> - user has create device access to this portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_contac&quot;</code> - user has receive alerts access from this portal.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get user portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li>Returned if the portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals/2123755496&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:45:53 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Length: 168 Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;PortalName&quot;: &quot;demo1&quot;, &quot;PortalID&quot;: &quot;2123755496&quot;, &quot;PortalRID&quot;: &quot;2c233ace8411c2af9b51b23985f86da23c732c00&quot;, &quot;UserEmail&quot;: &quot;demo@gmail.com&quot;, &quot;Description&quot;: &quot;Default Portal&quot;, &quot;Permissions&quot;: [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot; } ] } ] </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-permission">Get user permission</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/permissions</code></p> <p>Get the user&#39;s permissions.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own permissions.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="query-string">Query String</h5> <table> <thead> <tr> <th style="text-align:left">String</th> <th style="text-align:left">Description</th> <th style="text-align:left">Example</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td style="text-align:left"><code>type</code></td> <td style="text-align:left">is an array of permission types to retrieve. The supported types are <code>Domain</code>, <code>Portal</code>, <code>Device</code>, <code>DataSource</code>, and <code>Group</code>.</td> <td style="text-align:left"><code>users/{user-id}/permissions?type%5B%5D=Group</code> (Square brackets ([ and ]) are replaced with %5B and %5D respectively)</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with a body containing an array of <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> if get user&#39;s permissions successful.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user&#39;s permission.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/permissions?type%5B%5D=Portal&amp;type%5B%5D=Domain&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Mon, 17 Nov 2014 08:45:53 GMT Status: 200 OK Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 [ { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Domain&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;1231234567&quot; } }, { &quot;access&quot;: &quot;___admin&quot;, &quot;oid&quot;: { &quot;type&quot;: &quot;Portal&quot;, &quot;id&quot;: &quot;2490770768&quot; } } ] </code></pre><h4 id="add-user-permission">Add user permission</h4> <p><code>POST /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/permissions</code></p> <p>Add one or many <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> to user.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> <li>User must have access to the <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>The request body is an array <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned if add user permissions is successful.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have access to the <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to add permission to callee user.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> already exists in callee user permissions.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/permissions&#39; \ -X POST \ -d &#39;[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_u_list&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;1576946496&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Domain&quot;}}]&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:48:23 GMT Status: 202 Accepted Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/permissions Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="delete-user-permission">Delete user permission</h4> <p><code>DELETE /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/permissions</code></p> <p>Delete one or many <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> on user.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <ul> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> <li>User must have access to the <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>The request body is an array <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>204 No Content</code>: Returned if the user permissions is deleted successfully.</li> <li><code>400 Bad Request</code>: Returned if request body is invalid.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to delete user permissions.</li> <li>Returned if the <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> was deleted by other user and the callee user no longer has permissions on the object(s)</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if the <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a> was deleted by the callee user and the user no longer has permissions on the object(s).</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/permissions&#39; \ -X DELETE \ -d &#39;[{&quot;access&quot;:&quot;d_u_list&quot;,&quot;oid&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;1576946496&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Domain&quot;}}]&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 204 No Content Date: Tue, 18 Nov 2014 02:48:23 GMT Status: 204 No Content Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/permissions Vary: Accept-Encoding Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8 </code></pre><h4 id="get-user-profile-picture">Get user profile picture</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/profile/picture</code></p> <p>Get the user&#39;s profile picture.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his own profile picture.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty or picture.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned if getting the user&#39;s profile picture was successful. The picture had previously been uploaded by user and was returned within the body of the request.</li> <li><code>303 See Other</code>: Returned if getting the user&#39;s profile picture was successful and the profile picture was system default picture. The picture can be retrieved from the returned URL.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get callee user&#39;s permission.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/profile/picture&#39; \ -u &#39;useremail@gmail.com:userP4ssword&#39; \ -i </code></pre><pre><code>HTTP/1.1 303 See Other Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 06:21:16 GMT Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 Location: https://mydomain.exosite.com/static/png/user-64x64.png </code></pre><p>or</p> <pre><code>HTTP/1.1 200 OK Date: Fri, 22 May 2015 06:31:31 GMT Content-Type: image/png Transfer-Encoding: chunked Connection: keep-alive Keep-Alive: timeout=2 ▒PNG IHDR%▒V▒PLTEA▒▒▒▒V▒ IDATx▒cb67|▒IEND▒B`▒ </code></pre><h4 id="get-all-users-portals-shares">Get all users portals shares</h4> <p><code>GET /api/portals/v1/users/{user-id}/portals/shares</code></p> <p>Get user own portals and portal shares information.</p> <h5 id="permissions">Permissions</h5> <p>One of the following:</p> <ul> <li>User can get his portals and portal shares information.</li> <li>User must have at least <code>d_u_view</code> <a href="#permission-object">permission</a> to the domain.</li> </ul> <h5 id="request">Request</h5> <ul> <li>Request body is empty.</li> <li>Requires authentication.</li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>200 OK</code>: Returned along with an array of portal object if the caller has permission to get the user portal shares information. Portal objects contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;PortalName&quot;</code> - Portal name</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalID&quot;</code> - Portal ID</li> <li><code>&quot;PortalRID&quot;</code> - Portal RID</li> <li><code>&quot;UserEmail&quot;</code> - The portal’s direct owner&#39;s email</li> <li><code>&quot;Description&quot;</code> - Portal description</li> <li><code>&quot;shares&quot;</code> - Containing the information of users who are being shared with this portal. Shares object contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;access&quot;</code> - User’s permission for this portal. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;p_manage&quot;</code> - user has manager access to this portal. This permission grants the same rights as owner.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_m_crea&quot;</code> - user has create device access to this portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_contac&quot;</code> - user has receive alerts access from this portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;oid&quot;</code> - The information of the user. The object contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> - Id of the user who are being shared with this portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;type&quot;</code> - The general value is <strong>User</strong>.</li> <li><code>&quot;email&quot;</code> - Email of the user who are being shared with this portal.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to get user portal shares information.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals/shares&#39; The object contain the following keys:</p> <ul> <li><code>&quot;access&quot;</code> - User’s permission for this portal. Possible values are:<ul> <li><code>&quot;p_manage&quot;</code> - user has manager access to this portal. This permission grants the same rights as owner.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_m_crea&quot;</code> - user has create device access to this portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;p_contac&quot;</code> - user has receive alerts access from this portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>&quot;oid&quot;</code> - The information of the user. The object contain the following keys:<ul> <li><code>&quot;id&quot;</code> - Id of the user who are being shared with this portal.</li> <li><code>&quot;type&quot;</code> - The general value is <strong>User</strong>.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> </li> <li><p>Requires authentication.</p> </li> </ul> <h5 id="response">Response</h5> <ul> <li><code>202 Accepted</code>: Returned along with portal shares information if shares portal successfully.</li> <li><code>403 Forbidden</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the caller user is not authenticated.</li> <li>Returned if the caller user does not have permission to share the portal.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>404 Not Found</code>: one of the following:<ul> <li>Returned if the user id is invalid.</li> <li>Returned if the portal id is invalid.</li> </ul> </li> <li><code>409 Conflict</code>: Returned if the portal has already shared to the user in <a href="#permission-object">permission objects</a>.</li> </ul> <h5 id="example">Example</h5> <pre><code>curl &#39;https://mydomain.exosite.com/api/portals/v1/users/3167859736/portals/1173271281/shares&#39;
